\u00a0built \u00a0a \u00a0text-to-text_api \u00a0prompt \u00a0enhancement\r\nframework \u00a0called \u00a0TALM. \u00a0The \u00a0TALM \u00a0bootstrap \u00a0LLM \u00a0generates\r\n\u201c|tool-call\u201d\u00a0and\u00a0\u201ctool\u00a0input\u00a0text\u201d\u00a0to\u00a0construct\u00a0API\u00a0call\u00a0requests,\u00a0and\r\nthen \u00a0appends \u00a0the \u00a0text\r\nsequence,\u00a0significantly\u00a0expanding\u00a0the\u00a0model\u2019s\u00a0capabilities.\u00a0Similar\u00a0to\r\nthis, \u00a0Toolformer \u00a0[116] \u00a0uses \u00a0the \u00a0same \u00a0approach \u00a0of \u00a0including \u00a0API\r\nrequests\u00a0in\u00a0the\u00a0prompts\u00a0to\u00a0leave\u00a0the\u00a0sub-operations\u00a0to\u00a0external\u00a0tools,\r\nwhile\u00a0Toolformer\u00a0also\u00a0suggests\u00a0ways\u00a0to\u00a0build\u00a0datasets\u00a0and\u00a0fine-tune\r\nthem.\u00a0Galactica\u00a0[117]\u00a0adopts\u00a0a\u00a0special\u00a0token\u00a0to\u00a0initiate\u00a0a\u00a0request\u00a0to\r\ncall \u00a0an \u00a0external \u00a0tool. \u00a0This \u00a0work \u00a0delivers \u00a0the \u00a0concept \u00a0of\u00a0 \u201cwork\r\nmemory\u201d, \u00a0which \u00a0generates \u00a0a \u00a0special \u00a0segment \u00a0in \u00a0which \u00a0algorithms\r\nand \u00a0problem-solving \u00a0code \u00a0are \u00a0generated \u00a0when \u00a0the \u00a0model \u00a0needs \u00a0to\r\ncall\u00a0an\u00a0external\u00a0tool.\u00a0These\u00a0methods\u00a0require\u00a0a\u00a0strategy\u00a0to\u00a0determine\r\nwhat\u00a0tasks\u00a0should\u00a0be\u00a0offloaded.\r\nTo \u00a0overcome \u00a0the \u00a0limitations \u00a0of \u00a0manually \u00a0writing \u00a0API \u00a0requests,\r\nsome\u00a0works\u00a0provide\u00a0strategies\u00a0to\u00a0make\u00a0LLM\u00a0use\u00a0tools\u00a0automatically.\r\nMRKL \u00a0[118] \u00a0provides \u00a0a \u00a0modular \u00a0neural-symbolic \u00a0architecture \u00a0that\r\ndivides \u00a0tasks \u00a0into \u00a0corresponding \u00a0task \u00a0APIs \u00a0through \u00a0a \u00a0router \u00a0and\r\nintegrates\u00a0the\u00a0returned\u00a0results.\u00a0ART\u00a0[119]\u00a0organizes\u00a0its\u00a0task\u00a0library,\r\nretrieves\u00a0tasks\u00a0related\u00a0to\u00a0the\u00a0original\u00a0prompt\u00a0in\u00a0the\u00a0task\u00a0library,\u00a0then\r\ndecomposes \u00a0a \u00a0series \u00a0of \u00a0tasks \u00a0in \u00a0turn \u00a0into \u00a0corresponding \u00a0sub-tool\r\nsequences,\u00a0generates\u00a0a\u00a0specific\u00a0cue\u00a0word\u00a0to\u00a0be\u00a0processed,\u00a0and\u00a0finally\r\nintegrates \u00a0the \u00a0results \u00a0of \u00a0the \u00a0tool \u00a0API \u00a0into \u00a0the \u00a0original \u00a0cue \u00a0word \u00a0to\r\nrealize \u00a0the \u00a0automated \u00a0tool \u00a0usage \u00a0of \u00a0LLM. \u00a0More \u00a0large-scale\r\narchitectures\u00a0such\u00a0as\u00a0Chameleon\u00a0[120],\u00a0Gorilla\u00a0[121],\u00a0HuggingGPT\r\n[122],\u00a0and\u00a0ToolAlpaca\u00a0[123]\u00a0take\u00a0advantage\u00a0of\u00a0richer\u00a0API\u00a0tools\u00a0and\r\nmore\u00a0systematic\u00a0API\u00a0requests,\u00a0greatly\u00a0enhancing\u00a0the\u00a0ability\u00a0of\u00a0LLM\r\nto \u00a0use \u00a0tools \u00a0to \u00a0handle \u00a0tasks. \u00a0Based \u00a0on \u00a0these \u00a0architectures, \u00a0several\r\n\u201cLLM \u00a0+ \u00a0Tool\u201d\u00a0 agents \u00a0such \u00a0as \u00a0TPTU \u00a0[124], \u00a0TPTUv2 \u00a0[125], \u00a0and\r\nTaskMatrix. \u00a0AI \u00a0[126] \u00a0have \u00a0also \u00a0demonstrated \u00a0a \u00a0strong \u00a0ability \u00a0to\r\nhandle\u00a0complex\u00a0tasks\u00a0in\u00a0different\u00a0scenarios.\r\n\u25cf \u00a0Feedback. \u00a0Similar \u00a0to \u00a0human \u00a0learning \u00a0processes, \u00a0feedback\r\nenables \u00a0individuals \u00a0to \u00a0identify \u00a0areas \u00a0for \u00a0improvement \u00a0and \u00a0resolve\r\nissues\u00a0more\u00a0effectively.\u00a0The\u00a0provision\u00a0of\u00a0feedback\u00a0enables\u00a0the\u00a0LLM\r\nto \u00a0ascertain \u00a0the \u00a0correct \u00a0and \u00a0incorrect \u00a0responses \u00a0through \u00a0prompting,\r\nthereby\u00a0enhancing\u00a0its\u00a0capacity\u00a0for\u00a0reasoning.\u00a0In\u00a0accordance\u00a0with\u00a0the\r\nsubject\u00a0of\u00a0the\u00a0judgment,\u00a0feedback\u00a0can\u00a0be\u00a0classified\u00a0into\u00a0two\u00a0distinct\r\ncategories:\u00a0internal\u00a0feedback\u00a0and\u00a0external\u00a0feedback.\r\n(i) \u00a0Internal \u00a0feedback. \u00a0LLMs \u00a0possess \u00a0the \u00a0inherent \u00a0capability \u00a0to\r\nengage \u00a0in \u00a0self-feedback. \u00a0Numerous \u00a0scholars \u00a0in \u00a0this \u00a0field \u00a0have\r\ndemonstrated \u00a0the \u00a0self-feedback \u00a0ability \u00a0of \u00a0LLMs \u00a0and \u00a0have \u00a0proposed\r\ncorresponding \u00a0methods \u00a0to \u00a0enhance \u00a0and \u00a0leverage \u00a0this \u00a0mechanism\r\neffectively.\u00a0By\u00a0harnessing\u00a0self-feedback,\u00a0LLMs\u00a0can\u00a0iteratively\u00a0refine\r\ntheir\u00a0outputs,\u00a0contributing\u00a0to\u00a0their\u00a0continual\u00a0improvement\u00a0and\u00a0better\r\nperformance.\r\nInternal feedback techniques.\u00a0 Some \u00a0scholars \u00a0[127] \u00a0demonstrated\r\nthat \u00a0LLMs \u00a0can \u00a0undergo \u00a0iterative \u00a0self-refinement \u00a0without \u00a0requiring\r\nadditional \u00a0training, \u00a0introducing \u00a0the \u00a0SELF-REFINE \u00a0approach. \u00a0This\r\nmethod\u00a0refines\u00a0the\u00a0output\u00a0of\u00a0LLMs\u00a0through\u00a0alternating\u00a0iterations\u00a0of\r\nfeedback\u00a0and\u00a0refinement\u00a0to\u00a0enhance\u00a0the\u00a0output\u00a0quality.\u00a0The\u00a0feedback\r\ngeneration \u00a0process \u00a0is \u00a0guided \u00a0by \u00a0a \u00a0few-shot \u00a0prompt \u00a0[13]. \u00a0SELF\u0002REFINE \u00a0outperforms \u00a0models \u00a0such \u00a0as \u00a0GPT-3.5 \u00a0and \u00a0GPT-4, \u00a0directly\r\nyielding \u00a0absolute \u00a0improvements \u00a0ranging \u00a0from \u00a05%\u00a0 to \u00a040%. \u00a0In \u00a0tasks\r\ninvolving\u00a0code\u00a0generation,\u00a0when\u00a0applied\u00a0to\u00a0CODEX,\u00a0SELF-REFINE\r\nimproves\u00a0initial\u00a0generation\u00a0by\u00a0up\u00a0to\u00a013%.\r\nSELF \u00a0(Self-Evolution \u00a0with \u00a0Language \u00a0Feedback) \u00a0[128] \u00a0enables\r\nLLMs \u00a0to \u00a0engage \u00a0in \u00a0self-feedback \u00a0and \u00a0self-refinement. \u00a0This \u00a0is\r\nachieved \u00a0by \u00a0providing \u00a0LLMs \u00a0with \u00a0feedback \u00a0in \u00a0natural \u00a0language,\r\nempowering \u00a0them \u00a0to \u00a0autonomously \u00a0evolve. \u00a0The \u00a0evolution \u00a0process\r\ninvolves \u00a0generating \u00a0responses \u00a0to \u00a0unlabeled \u00a0instructions \u00a0and\r\niteratively \u00a0refining \u00a0these \u00a0responses \u00a0through \u00a0interactions. \u00a0SELF\r\nteaches \u00a0LLMs \u00a0fundamental \u00a0meta-skills \u00a0using \u00a0a \u00a0limited \u00a0set \u00a0of\r\nexamples \u00a0in \u00a0natural \u00a0language, \u00a0fostering \u00a0a \u00a0continuous \u00a0cycle \u00a0of \u00a0self\u0002evolution\u00a0for\u00a0LLMs.\u00a0Self-Contrast\u00a0[129]\u00a0enhances\u00a0the\u00a0self-feedback\r\ncapacity\u00a0of\u00a0LLMs.\u00a0This\u00a0approach\u00a0prompts\u00a0LLMs\u00a0to\u00a0generate\u00a0various\r\nperspectives \u00a0to \u00a0address \u00a0the \u00a0same \u00a0problem, \u00a0subsequently \u00a0facilitating\r\ncomparison \u00a0and \u00a0reflection \u00a0on \u00a0the \u00a0disparities \u00a0among \u00a0these\r\nperspectives.\r\nSome \u00a0scholars \u00a0[130] \u00a0proposed \u00a0that \u00a0LLMs \u00a0can \u00a0autonomously\r\nprovide\u00a0self-feedback\u00a0regarding\u00a0hyperparameter\u00a0perception.\u00a0Through\r\nhyperparameter-aware\u00a0instruction\u00a0tuning,\u00a0LLMs\u00a0ascertain\u00a0the\u00a0optimal\r\ndecoding\u00a0strategy\u00a0and\u00a0configuration\u00a0based\u00a0on\u00a0input\u00a0samples,\u00a0thereby\r\nachieving \u00a0self-regulation. \u00a0Their \u00a0proposed \u00a0HAG \u00a0(Hyperparameter\r\nAware\u00a0Generation)\u00a0consists\u00a0of\u00a0two\u00a0components.\u00a0Firstly,\u00a0by\u00a0inputting\r\na\u00a0query\u00a0Q\u00a0to\u00a0the\u00a0LLM,\u00a0HAG\u00a0generates\u00a0appropriate\u00a0hyperparameters.\r\nSubsequently, \u00a0HAG \u00a0instructs \u00a0the \u00a0LLM \u00a0to \u00a0adjust \u00a0the \u00a0model\u2019s\r\ndecoding\u00a0strategies\u00a0and\u00a0hyperparameters\u00a0according\u00a0to\u00a0the\u00a0generated\r\nparameters, \u00a0culminating \u00a0in \u00a0the \u00a0generation \u00a0of \u00a0the \u00a0final \u00a0result \u00a0post\u0002adjustment.\r\nEvaluation of internal feedback. For \u00a0the \u00a0evaluation \u00a0of \u00a0internal\r\nfeedback, \u00a0some \u00a0scholars \u00a0[131] \u00a0proposed \u00a0that \u00a0glass-box \u00a0features\r\nshould \u00a0be \u00a0taken \u00a0into \u00a0account \u00a0in \u00a0self-assessment \u00a0of \u00a0LLMs. \u00a0They\r\nproposed \u00a0that \u00a0the \u00a0softmax \u00a0distribution \u00a0serves \u00a0as \u00a0a \u00a0dependable\r\nindicator \u00a0for \u00a0quality \u00a0evaluation. \u00a0Self-feedback \u00a0can \u00a0enhance\r\nperformance\u00a0on\u00a0certain\u00a0tasks\u00a0for\u00a0LLMs,\u00a0while\u00a0potentially\u00a0worsening\r\nperformance \u00a0on \u00a0others \u00a0[132]. \u00a0In \u00a0light \u00a0of \u00a0this, \u00a0some \u00a0scholars \u00a0[133]\r\nintroduced \u00a0the \u00a0concept \u00a0of \u00a0Self-Bias \u00a0to \u00a0evaluate \u00a0the \u00a0bias \u00a0of \u00a0LLM\r\noutput \u00a0accuracy \u00a0across \u00a0different \u00a0tasks. \u00a0Additionally, \u00a0their \u00a0research\r\nreveals \u00a0that \u00a0models \u00a0with \u00a0larger \u00a0parameters \u00a0and \u00a0access \u00a0to \u00a0external\r\nfeedback \u00a0possess \u00a0the \u00a0ability \u00a0to \u00a0more \u00a0accurately \u00a0assess \u00a0and \u00a0mitigate\r\nSelf-Bias.\r\n(ii) \u00a0External \u00a0feedback. \u00a0Certain \u00a0external \u00a0tools \u00a0can \u00a0verify \u00a0the\r\nextrapolation \u00a0outputs \u00a0of \u00a0LLMs. \u00a0CRITIC \u00a0framework \u00a0[134] \u00a0enables\r\nappropriate\u00a0tools\u00a0to\u00a0assess\u00a0the\u00a0output\u00a0of\u00a0LLMs,\u00a0which\u00a0in\u00a0turn\u00a0allows\r\nLLMs\u00a0to\u00a0adjust\u00a0and\u00a0refine\u00a0their\u00a0output\u00a0based\u00a0on\u00a0this\u00a0feedback.\u00a0These\r\nexternal \u00a0evaluation \u00a0tools \u00a0encompass \u00a0search \u00a0engines, \u00a0code\r\ninterpreters, \u00a0text \u00a0APIs, \u00a0and \u00a0more. \u00a0The \u00a0feedback \u00a0process \u00a0primarily\r\ninvolves \u00a0validating \u00a0the \u00a0initial \u00a0output \u00a0expectations \u00a0generated \u00a0by \u00a0the\r\nLLMs \u00a0and \u00a0then \u00a0modifying \u00a0the \u00a0output \u00a0based \u00a0on \u00a0critiques \u00a0from \u00a0the\r\nverification \u00a0process. \u00a0Through \u00a0this \u00a0iterative \u00a0process, \u00a0external \u00a0tools\r\noffer \u00a0feedback \u00a0to \u00a0LLMs \u00a0from \u00a0an \u00a0external \u00a0perspective, \u00a0thereby\r\nenhancing\u00a0the\u00a0performance\u00a0of\u00a0LLMs.\r\nYao-Yang\u00a0LIU\u00a0et\u00a0al.\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0A\u00a0comprehensive\u00a0taxonomy\u00a0of\u00a0prompt\u00a0engineering\u00a0techniques\u00a0for\u00a0large\u00a0language\u00a0models\r\nFrontiers of Computer Science\u00a0\u00a0|\u00a0Issue\u00a03\u00a0|\u00a0Volume\u00a020\u00a0|\u00a0March\u00a02026\u00a0|\u00a02003601-10\n3.4\u00a0\u00a0Reliability\r\nIn \u00a0the \u00a0first \u00a0three \u00a0parts, \u00a0we \u00a0introduce \u00a0how \u00a0to \u00a0design \u00a0an \u00a0effective\r\nprompt \u00a0for \u00a0LLMs \u00a0using \u00a0the \u00a0Profile-Knowledge-Reasoning \u00a0process.\r\nDue\u00a0to\u00a0the\u00a0uncertainty\u00a0of\u00a0the\u00a0LLM\u2019s\u00a0response\u00a0[135],\u00a0the\u00a0same\u00a0prompt\r\ncan\u00a0lead\u00a0to\u00a0diversified\u00a0responses\u00a0from\u00a0the\u00a0LLM.\u00a0At\u00a0the\u00a0same\u00a0time,\r\ndue\u00a0to\u00a0the\u00a0LLM\u2019s\u00a0context\u00a0learning\u00a0ability,\u00a0it\u00a0is\u00a0particularly\u00a0sensitive\r\nto\u00a0the\u00a0order,\u00a0type,\u00a0and\u00a0historical\u00a0bias\u00a0of\u00a0the\u00a0prompts\u00a0[135\u2013137].\u00a0The\r\nbias \u00a0of \u00a0the \u00a0prompt \u00a0may \u00a0worsen \u00a0the \u00a0performance \u00a0of \u00a0the \u00a0LLM \u00a0in\r\ndownstream \u00a0tasks. \u00a0Furthermore, \u00a0the \u00a0reasoning \u00a0strategy \u00a0used \u00a0by \u00a0the\r\nLLM\u00a0is\u00a0opaque,\u00a0which\u00a0means\u00a0that\u00a0the\u00a0responses\u00a0of\u00a0the\u00a0LLM\u00a0are\u00a0not\r\nalways \u00a0trustworthy \u00a0[138], \u00a0and \u00a0there \u00a0are \u00a0a \u00a0series \u00a0of \u00a0risks \u00a0associated\r\nwith\u00a0the\u00a0responses\u00a0of\u00a0the\u00a0LLM\u00a0[139,140].\u00a0In\u00a0practical\u00a0applications,\r\nusers\u00a0often\u00a0demand\u00a0stable\u00a0and\u00a0reliable\u00a0responses\u00a0from\u00a0the\u00a0LLM.\u00a0The\r\nprocess\u00a0of\u00a0reducing\u00a0the\u00a0bias\u00a0of\u00a0the\u00a0LLM\u2019s\u00a0response\u00a0through\u00a0prompt\r\nintegration \u00a0or \u00a0by \u00a0generating \u00a0auxiliary \u00a0knowledge \u00a0from \u00a0the \u00a0LLM \u00a0is\r\nknown\u00a0as\u00a0improving\u00a0the\u00a0reliability\u00a0of\u00a0the\u00a0LLM.\u00a0In\u00a0this\u00a0part,\u00a0we\u00a0will\r\nexplain\u00a0from\u00a0both\u00a0perspectives\u00a0of\u00a0content\u00a0bias\u00a0and\u00a0value\u00a0bias.\r\n1)\u00a0Content\u00a0bias\r\nWe \u00a0define \u00a0content \u00a0bias \u00a0as \u00a0the \u00a0deviation \u00a0between \u00a0the \u00a0completion\r\nresults\u00a0of\u00a0the\u00a0LLM\u00a0and\u00a0the\u00a0task\u00a0requirements.\u00a0For\u00a0most\u00a0LLM\u00a0tasks,\r\ndesigning \u00a0prompts \u00a0according \u00a0to \u00a0the \u00a0profile-knowledge-reasoning\r\nprocess \u00a0can \u00a0help \u00a0the \u00a0LLM \u00a0perform \u00a0well \u00a0in \u00a0response \u00a0to \u00a0task\r\nrequirements.\u00a0However,\u00a0when\u00a0the\u00a0task\u00a0is\u00a0more\u00a0complex,\u00a0it\u00a0is\u00a0difficult\r\nto\u00a0obtain\u00a0stable\u00a0and\u00a0perfect\u00a0output\u00a0through\u00a0a\u00a0single\u00a0round\u00a0of\u00a0prompt\r\ninput \u00a0[137,139]. \u00a0An \u00a0intuitive \u00a0idea \u00a0is \u00a0to \u00a0adjust \u00a0the \u00a0order \u00a0of \u00a0the\r\nprompts \u00a0or \u00a0change \u00a0the \u00a0method \u00a0of \u00a0prompting \u00a0to \u00a0generate \u00a0multiple\r\nrounds \u00a0for \u00a0the \u00a0same \u00a0question, \u00a0which \u00a0actually \u00a0uses \u00a0the \u00a0concept \u00a0of\r\nensemble. \u00a0The \u00a0prompt \u00a0method \u00a0based \u00a0on \u00a0this \u00a0idea \u00a0is \u00a0called \u00a0prompt\r\nensembling.\r\nPrompt\u00a0ensembling\u00a0refers\u00a0to\u00a0the\u00a0use\u00a0of\u00a0multiple\u00a0different\u00a0prompts\r\nto \u00a0complete \u00a0the \u00a0same \u00a0task, \u00a0enhancing \u00a0the \u00a0reliability \u00a0of \u00a0the \u00a0results\r\nthrough \u00a0multiple \u00a0responses. \u00a0Prompt \u00a0ensembling \u00a0borrows \u00a0from \u00a0the\r\npattern \u00a0of \u00a0ensemble \u00a0learning \u00a0and \u00a0includes \u00a0two \u00a0sub-processes: \u00a0first\r\ngenerating \u00a0multiple \u00a0prompts \u00a0as \u00a0input, \u00a0and \u00a0then \u00a0combining \u00a0the\r\nresponses \u00a0of \u00a0multiple \u00a0prompts \u00a0through \u00a0a \u00a0specific \u00a0strategy \u00a0to \u00a0obtain\r\nthe \u00a0final \u00a0result \u00a0[141,142]. \u00a0Bagging \u00a0and \u00a0boosting \u00a0are \u00a0two \u00a0typical\r\nensemble \u00a0methods \u00a0widely \u00a0used \u00a0in \u00a0many \u00a0classic \u00a0tasks \u00a0and \u00a0have\r\nunique\u00a0applications\u00a0in\u00a0LLM.\r\n\u25cf \u00a0Bagging \u00a0prompt. \u00a0The \u00a0application \u00a0of \u00a0Bagging \u00a0Prompt \u00a0in \u00a0LLM\r\nmainly\u00a0falls\u00a0into\u00a0two\u00a0categories:\u00a0the\u00a0majority\u00a0vote\u00a0method\u00a0based\u00a0on\r\nSelf-Consistency\u00a0[143]\u00a0and\u00a0the\u00a0beam\u00a0search\u00a0method\u00a0based\u00a0on\u00a0Step\u0002Verifier \u00a0[144]. \u00a0BPE \u00a0[145] \u00a0focuses \u00a0on \u00a0constructing \u00a0few-shot \u00a0CoT\r\nprompts \u00a0based \u00a0on \u00a0Self-Consistency, \u00a0which \u00a0outperforms \u00a0a \u00a0single\r\nprompt. \u00a0However, \u00a0since \u00a0Self-Consistency \u00a0is \u00a0a \u00a0method \u00a0based \u00a0on \u00a0a\r\ngreedy \u00a0approach, \u00a0it \u00a0cannot \u00a0guarantee \u00a0that \u00a0the \u00a0inference \u00a0chain \u00a0is\r\nentirely \u00a0correct. \u00a0Additionally, \u00a0its \u00a0voting \u00a0mechanism \u00a0is \u00a0atomic,\r\nmeaning\u00a0it\u00a0lacks\u00a0the\u00a0ability\u00a0to\u00a0differentiate\u00a0the\u00a0quality\u00a0among\u00a0various\r\nresponses.\r\nIn\u00a0response\u00a0to\u00a0these\u00a0challenges,\u00a0DiVeRSe\u00a0[146]\u00a0was\u00a0developed\u00a0to\r\nenhance\u00a0answer\u00a0reliability\u00a0through\u00a0a\u00a0three-stage\u00a0process:\u00a0 \u201cgenerate\u0002verify-check\u201d.\u00a0First,\u00a0it\u00a0generates\u00a0diverse\u00a0completions\u00a0using\u00a0multiple\r\nprompts. \u00a0Next, \u00a0a\u00a0 \u201cstep-aware \u00a0voting \u00a0verifier\u201d\u00a0 model \u00a0distinguishes\r\ngood \u00a0answers \u00a0from \u00a0poor \u00a0ones \u00a0and \u00a0verifies \u00a0the \u00a0correctness \u00a0of\r\ninference\u00a0steps.\u00a0DiVeRSe\u00a0extends\u00a0traditional\u00a0methods\u00a0by\u00a0extracting\r\nstep-level\u00a0labels\u00a0from\u00a0intermediate\u00a0results,\u00a0ensuring\u00a0accuracy\u00a0in\u00a0the\r\ninference \u00a0flow. \u00a0While \u00a0it \u00a0integrates \u00a0the \u00a0benefits \u00a0of \u00a0bagging \u00a0Prompt\r\nmethods, \u00a0DiVeRSe \u00a0still \u00a0relies \u00a0on \u00a0manual \u00a0sample \u00a0selection, \u00a0and\r\nsample\u00a0bias\u00a0can\u00a0affect\u00a0final\u00a0results.\r\nMotivated\u00a0by\u00a0these\u00a0issues,\u00a0the\u00a0AMA\u00a0(Ask\u00a0Me\u00a0Anything)\u00a0method\r\nwas \u00a0introduced \u00a0[147]. \u00a0AMA \u00a0consists \u00a0of \u00a0two \u00a0stages: \u00a0the \u00a0multiple\r\nprompt\u00a0step\u00a0and\u00a0the\u00a0answer\u00a0aggregation\u00a0step.\u00a0In\u00a0the\u00a0multiple\u00a0prompt\r\nstep,\u00a0AMA\u00a0employs\u00a0a\u00a0functional\u00a0prompt\u00a0chain\u00a0where\u00a0the\u00a0question()\r\nfunction \u00a0transforms \u00a0the \u00a0input \u00a0into \u00a0open-ended \u00a0questions, \u00a0providing\r\ndiverse \u00a0perspectives \u00a0for \u00a0LLMs \u00a0to \u00a0address \u00a0different \u00a0aspects \u00a0of \u00a0the\r\nproblem.\u00a0The\u00a0answer()\u00a0function\u00a0then\u00a0generates\u00a0intermediate\u00a0answers.\r\nAMA \u00a0highlights \u00a0the \u00a0limitations \u00a0of \u00a0simple \u00a0voting \u00a0due \u00a0to \u00a0equal\r\nweighting \u00a0and \u00a0question \u00a0similarity, \u00a0which \u00a0can \u00a0distort \u00a0results. \u00a0To\r\novercome \u00a0this, \u00a0AMA \u00a0uses \u00a0an \u00a0answer \u00a0aggregation \u00a0method \u00a0based \u00a0on\r\nweakly \u00a0supervised \u00a0learning \u00a0with \u00a0an \u00a0information \u00a0entropy \u00a0penalty,\r\nensuring\u00a0that\u00a0results\u00a0better\u00a0reflect\u00a0different\u00a0perspectives.\u00a0Essentially,\r\nAMA\u00a0optimizes\u00a0the\u00a0Bagging\u00a0random\u00a0sampling\u00a0approach.\r\n\u25cf\u00a0Boosting\u00a0prompt.\u00a0Boosting\u00a0prompt\u00a0methods\u00a0often\u00a0adopt\u00a0a\u00a0two\u0002stage \u00a0paradigm. \u00a0PromptBoosting \u00a0[148] \u00a0applies \u00a0the \u00a0AdaBoost\r\nalgorithm \u00a0on \u00a0the \u00a0prompt \u00a0set, \u00a0achieving \u00a0good \u00a0results \u00a0in \u00a0text\r\nclassification. \u00a0However, \u00a0the \u00a0PromptBoosting \u00a0method \u00a0requires \u00a0a\r\nprepared \u00a0high-quality \u00a0prompt \u00a0set \u00a0and \u00a0cannot \u00a0optimize \u00a0for \u00a0specific\r\nprompts.\r\nTo\u00a0overcome\u00a0these\u00a0limitations,\u00a0Prefer\u00a0[149]\u00a0establishes\u00a0a\u00a0feedback\r\nmechanism\u00a0to\u00a0reflect\u00a0on\u00a0the\u00a0shortcomings\u00a0of\u00a0the\u00a0weak\u00a0learners\u00a0in\u00a0the\r\ncurrent \u00a0iteration. \u00a0Based \u00a0on \u00a0feedback, \u00a0Prefer \u00a0also \u00a0implements \u00a0the\r\nautomatic \u00a0synthesis \u00a0and \u00a0selection \u00a0of \u00a0prompts, \u00a0avoiding \u00a0the \u00a0bias\r\nproblem \u00a0brought \u00a0by \u00a0the \u00a0prompts. \u00a0PromptBoosting\u2019s \u00a0ensemble\r\nmethod\u00a0for\u00a0weak\u00a0learners\u00a0refers\u00a0to\u00a0the\u00a0traditional\u00a0ensemble\u00a0method\r\nof\u00a0weighted\u00a0summation.\u00a0However,\u00a0many\u00a0works\u00a0have\u00a0pointed\u00a0out\u00a0that\r\nLLMs\u00a0have\u00a0a\u00a0serious\u00a0optimistic\u00a0estimation\u00a0problem\u00a0[150,151].\u00a0This\r\nmakes \u00a0the \u00a0weighted \u00a0calculation \u00a0of \u00a0answer \u00a0accuracy \u00a0unable \u00a0to\r\neliminate\u00a0content\u00a0bias.\r\nBilateral \u00a0Prompt \u00a0Bagging \u00a0[149] \u00a0assesses \u00a0the \u00a0confidence \u00a0of \u00a0the\r\ngenerated\u00a0results\u00a0in\u00a0each\u00a0iteration.\u00a0When\u00a0the\u00a0assessment\u00a0result\u00a0of\u00a0the\r\nanswer \u00a0is \u00a0not \u00a0trustworthy, \u00a0a \u00a0reverse \u00a0confidence \u00a0evaluation \u00a0is\r\nperformed, \u00a0calculating \u00a0the \u00a0confidence \u00a0that \u00a0this \u00a0answer \u00a0is \u00a0incorrect.\r\nThe \u00a0final \u00a0correct \u00a0probability \u00a0of \u00a0a \u00a0round \u00a0of \u00a0generated \u00a0results \u00a0is\r\nevaluated\u00a0by\u00a0combining\u00a0forward\u00a0and\u00a0reverse\u00a0confidence.\u00a0This\u00a0design\r\nof\u00a0positive\u00a0and\u00a0negative\u00a0confidence\u00a0effectively\u00a0avoids\u00a0the\u00a0optimistic\r\nestimation \u00a0problem \u00a0of \u00a0LLMs \u00a0[150]. \u00a0By \u00a0leveraging \u00a0the \u00a0feedback\r\nreasoning \u00a0capabilities \u00a0of \u00a0LLMs \u00a0(as \u00a0discussed \u00a0in \u00a0Subsection \u00a02.3), \u00a0it\r\nenhances \u00a0the \u00a0quality \u00a0of \u00a0single-round \u00a0generated \u00a0results, \u00a0strengthens\r\nweak \u00a0learners, \u00a0and \u00a0ensures \u00a0a \u00a0more \u00a0reliable \u00a0and \u00a0efficient \u00a0final\r\noutcome.\r\n2)\u00a0Value\u00a0bias\r\nWe\u00a0define\u00a0value\u00a0bias\u00a0as\u00a0the\u00a0deviation\u00a0between\u00a0the\u00a0content\u00a0generated\r\nFront.\u00a0Comput.\u00a0Sci.,\u00a02026,\u00a020(3):\u00a02003601\r\nFrontiers of Computer Science\u00a0\u00a0|\u00a0Issue\u00a03\u00a0|\u00a0Volume\u00a020\u00a0|\u00a0March\u00a02026\u00a0|\u00a02003601-11\nby\u00a0LLMs\u00a0and\u00a0human\u00a0societal\u00a0values.\u00a0The\u00a0content\u00a0generated\u00a0by\u00a0LLMs\r\noften\u00a0touches\u00a0upon\u00a0socially\u00a0sensitive\u00a0areas,\u00a0such\u00a0as\u00a0issues\u00a0of\u00a0social\r\nharm\u00a0and\u00a0discrimination\u00a0[152,153].\u00a0Shaikh\u00a0et\u00a0al.\u00a0[139]\u00a0showed\u00a0that\r\nChain\u00a0of\u00a0Thought\u00a0(CoT)\u00a0can\u00a0continually\u00a0enhance\u00a0the\u00a0performance\u00a0of\r\nLLMs\u00a0across\u00a0a\u00a0variety\u00a0of\u00a0NLP\u00a0tasks.\u00a0However,\u00a0this\u00a0also\u00a0increases\u00a0the\r\nlikelihood \u00a0of \u00a0the \u00a0model \u00a0producing \u00a0harmful \u00a0or \u00a0inappropriate \u00a0results.\r\nResearch\u00a0[154]\u00a0indicates\u00a0that\u00a0CoT\u00a0prompts\u00a0should\u00a0be\u00a0used\u00a0carefully\r\nwhen\u00a0dealing\u00a0with\u00a0socially\u00a0relevant\u00a0issues.\u00a0Due\u00a0to\u00a0the\u00a0principles\u00a0of\r\nautoregressive \u00a0decoding \u00a0inherent \u00a0in \u00a0LLMs, \u00a0harmful \u00a0text \u00a0might \u00a0still\r\nbe\u00a0generated\u00a0during\u00a0the\u00a0beam-search\u00a0phase\u00a0of\u00a0the\u00a0inference\u00a0stage\u00a0if\r\nthe \u00a0volume \u00a0of \u00a0harmful \u00a0text \u00a0in \u00a0the \u00a0training \u00a0corpus \u00a0is \u00a0large \u00a0enough.\r\nThis\u00a0underlines\u00a0the\u00a0importance\u00a0of\u00a0developing\u00a0mechanisms\u00a0to\u00a0manage\r\nand \u00a0minimize \u00a0harmful \u00a0or \u00a0socially \u00a0unacceptable \u00a0outputs \u00a0for \u00a0the \u00a0safe\r\ndeployment\u00a0of\u00a0AI\u00a0systems.\r\nTang \u00a0et \u00a0al. \u00a0[155] \u00a0proposed \u00a0the \u00a0Detox-Chain \u00a0method, \u00a0which \u00a0links\r\ndetoxification \u00a0sub-steps \u00a0together \u00a0to \u00a0achieve \u00a0rapid \u00a0detoxification \u00a0of\r\nprompts. \u00a0The \u00a0Detox-Chain \u00a0method \u00a0reduces \u00a0the \u00a0possibility \u00a0of \u00a0LLM\r\ngenerating \u00a0toxic \u00a0texts \u00a0by \u00a0substituting \u00a0toxic \u00a0textual \u00a0representations.\r\nHowever, \u00a0due \u00a0to \u00a0the \u00a0detoxification \u00a0technology \u00a0for \u00a0prompts \u00a0altering\r\nthe\u00a0distribution\u00a0or\u00a0content\u00a0of\u00a0the\u00a0prompt\u00a0to\u00a0varying\u00a0extents,\u00a0it\u00a0affects\r\nthe\u00a0quality\u00a0of\u00a0the\u00a0output\u00a0produced\u00a0by\u00a0the\u00a0LLM.\u00a0At\u00a0the\u00a0current\u00a0stage,\r\nthe \u00a0detoxification \u00a0methods \u00a0for \u00a0LLMs \u00a0are \u00a0still \u00a0primarily \u00a0based \u00a0on\r\nreinforcement \u00a0learning \u00a0or \u00a0knowledge \u00a0editing \u00a0techniques \u00a0during \u00a0the\r\ntraining\u00a0phase.\r\n\u25a0 4 Applications\r\nThis\u00a0section\u00a0offers\u00a0practitioners\u00a0a\u00a0comprehensive\u00a0overview\u00a0of\u00a0current\r\napplication\u00a0domains\u00a0for\u00a0LLMs\u00a0and\u00a0highlights\u00a0the\u00a0prompt\u00a0engineering\r\ntechniques \u00a0utilized \u00a0across \u00a0diverse \u00a0use \u00a0cases. \u00a0While \u00a0existing \u00a0studies\r\n[156] \u00a0have \u00a0introduced \u00a0taxonomies \u00a0for \u00a0LLM \u00a0applications, \u00a0these\r\nclassifications \u00a0tend \u00a0to \u00a0focus \u00a0on \u00a0specific \u00a0scenarios, \u00a0limiting \u00a0their\r\nrelevance \u00a0for \u00a0prompt \u00a0engineering \u00a0design. \u00a0To \u00a0address \u00a0this \u00a0gap, \u00a0we\r\npropose \u00a0a \u00a0novel \u00a0taxonomy \u00a0that \u00a0categorizes \u00a0applications \u00a0by \u00a0task\r\ncharacteristics \u00a0into \u00a0two \u00a0primary \u00a0types: \u00a0cognitive \u00a0applications \u00a0and\r\ntransformative \u00a0applications \u00a0of \u00a0LLMs. \u00a0Cognitive \u00a0applications\r\nhighlight \u00a0LLMs\u2019\u00a0 roles \u00a0in \u00a0providing \u00a0and \u00a0processing \u00a0information,\r\nwhereas \u00a0transformative \u00a0applications \u00a0involve \u00a0tasks \u00a0where \u00a0LLMs\r\noperate \u00a0autonomously, \u00a0potentially \u00a0substituting \u00a0human \u00a0involvement.\r\nThis \u00a0taxonomy \u00a0provides \u00a0detailed \u00a0insights \u00a0into \u00a0prompt \u00a0engineering\r\ntechniques \u00a0tailored \u00a0for \u00a0each \u00a0application \u00a0category, \u00a0as \u00a0illustrated \u00a0in\r\nFig.\u00a01.\r\n4.1\u00a0\u00a0Cognitive\u00a0applications\u00a0of\u00a0LLMs\r\nCognitive \u00a0applications \u00a0of \u00a0LLMs \u00a0involve \u00a0utilizing \u00a0these \u00a0models \u00a0to\r\nacquire\u00a0and\u00a0analyze\u00a0information.\u00a0The\u00a0process\u00a0of\u00a0leveraging\u00a0LLMs\u00a0to\r\nextract \u00a0and \u00a0present \u00a0knowledge \u00a0is \u00a0termed \u00a0Information \u00a0Acquisition.\r\nThis \u00a0category \u00a0encompasses \u00a0applications \u00a0such \u00a0as \u00a0chatbots,\r\nprofessional \u00a0knowledge \u00a0Q&A, \u00a0search \u00a0engines, \u00a0and \u00a0training \u00a0data\r\naugmentation. \u00a0Conversely, \u00a0when \u00a0LLMs \u00a0are \u00a0employed \u00a0to \u00a0interpret\r\nand \u00a0analyze \u00a0input \u00a0data, \u00a0the \u00a0process \u00a0is \u00a0referred \u00a0to \u00a0as \u00a0In-depth\r\nInformation \u00a0Analysis. \u00a0Key \u00a0applications \u00a0in \u00a0this \u00a0analytical \u00a0domain\r\ninclude \u00a0the \u00a0simulation \u00a0of \u00a0financial \u00a0market \u00a0dynamics \u00a0and \u00a0the\r\nexploration\u00a0of\u00a0chemical\u00a0molecular\u00a0structures,\u00a0showcasing\u00a0the\u00a0model\u2019s\r\nability \u00a0to \u00a0provide \u00a0insightful \u00a0analyses \u00a0and \u00a0predictive \u00a0insights \u00a0across\r\nspecialized\u00a0fields.\r\n1)\u00a0Information\u00a0acquisition\r\nInformation \u00a0acquisition \u00a0is \u00a0a \u00a0fundamental \u00a0application \u00a0of \u00a0LLMs,\r\nleveraging \u00a0their \u00a0extensive \u00a0knowledge \u00a0base \u00a0to \u00a0efficiently \u00a0deliver\r\nrelevant\u00a0information\u00a0to\u00a0users.\r\n\u25cf \u00a0Chatbots. \u00a0General \u00a0chatbots, \u00a0also \u00a0known \u00a0as \u00a0dialogue \u00a0agents,\r\nintegrate \u00a0tasks \u00a0such \u00a0as \u00a0information \u00a0retrieval, \u00a0multi-turn \u00a0interaction,\r\nand \u00a0text \u00a0generation \u00a0(including \u00a0code). \u00a0LLMs \u00a0encapsulate \u00a0extensive\r\nknowledge\u00a0within\u00a0their\u00a0parameters\u00a0during\u00a0training.\u00a0Users\u00a0can\u00a0obtain\r\ninformation \u00a0from \u00a0LLMs \u00a0through \u00a0role-playing \u00a0dialogue, \u00a0exemplified\r\nby\u00a0the\u00a0chatbot\u00a0[157].\r\nFor \u00a0instance, \u00a0Glaese \u00a0et \u00a0al. \u00a0[158] \u00a0introduced \u00a0Sparrow, \u00a0a \u00a0dialogue\r\nagent\u00a0based\u00a0on\u00a0a\u00a070B\u00a0parameter\u00a0Chinchilla\u00a0LLM.\u00a0It\u00a0utilizes\u00a0prompt\r\nengineering \u00a0techniques, \u00a0including \u00a0Basic \u00a0RAG \u00a0Techniques\r\n(Subsection \u00a03.2) \u00a0and \u00a0Personality \u00a0Information \u00a0(Subsection \u00a03.1), \u00a0to\r\naddress\u00a0hallucination\u00a0issues\u00a0by\u00a0integrating\u00a0external\u00a0knowledge\u00a0from\r\nGoogle\u00a0search\u00a0queries.\r\nSimilarly,\u00a0OpenAI\u00a0[159]\u00a0utilizes\u00a0supervised\u00a0fine-tuning\u00a0with\u00a0high\u0002quality\u00a0data,\u00a0along\u00a0with\u00a0reinforcement\u00a0learning\u00a0from\u00a0human\u00a0feedback\r\n(RLHF),\u00a0to\u00a0develop\u00a0the\u00a0GPT-3.5\u00a0LLM,\u00a0which\u00a0powers\u00a0the\u00a0ChatGPT\r\nchatbot.\u00a0The\u00a0subsequent\u00a0GPT-4\u00a0model\u00a0[160]\u00a0underpins\u00a0the\u00a0ChatGPT\r\nPlus \u00a0chatbot. \u00a0ChatGPT \u00a0employs \u00a0prompt \u00a0techniques \u00a0such \u00a0as\r\nPersonality \u00a0Information \u00a0(Subsection \u00a03.1) \u00a0for \u00a0role-playing\r\nconversations\u00a0and\u00a0Memory\u00a0(Subsection\u00a03.2)\u00a0to\u00a0maintain\u00a0conversation\r\nhistory,\u00a0thereby\u00a0excelling\u00a0in\u00a0extended\u00a0discussions.\u00a0Microsoft\u00a0Copilot\r\n[161]\u00a0is\u00a0an\u00a0AI-powered\u00a0productivity\u00a0tool\u00a0that\u00a0integrates\u00a0an\u00a0LLM\u00a0with\r\nMicrosoft \u00a0365. \u00a0Supported \u00a0by \u00a0an \u00a0OpenAI \u00a0model, \u00a0Copilot \u00a0utilizes\r\nadditional \u00a0integration \u00a0tools \u00a0(Subsection \u00a03.3), \u00a0accesses \u00a0up-to-date\r\ninformation \u00a0via \u00a0Bing, \u00a0and \u00a0incorporates \u00a0Retrieval-Augmented\r\nGeneration \u00a0(RAG) \u00a0technology \u00a0(Subsection \u00a03.2) \u00a0to \u00a0enhance \u00a0user\r\nprompts.\r\nAnthropic \u00a0[162] \u00a0introduces \u00a0the \u00a0Claude \u00a0series \u00a0of \u00a0chatbots. \u00a0These\r\nbots \u00a0are \u00a0further \u00a0refined \u00a0via \u00a0fine-tuning \u00a0with \u00a0high-quality \u00a0data \u00a0and\r\nguided\u00a0by\u00a0RLHF\u00a0to\u00a0generate\u00a0responses\u00a0that\u00a0are\u00a0beneficial,\u00a0harmless,\r\nand \u00a0honest. \u00a0The \u00a0Claude \u00a03.5 \u00a0Sonnet \u00a0model \u00a0has \u00a0outperformed\r\ncompetitor \u00a0models \u00a0in \u00a0various \u00a0AI \u00a0system \u00a0evaluation \u00a0benchmarks,\r\nincluding\u00a0undergraduate-level\u00a0expert\u00a0knowledge\u00a0(MMLU),\u00a0graduate\u0002level\u00a0expert\u00a0reasoning\u00a0(GPQA),\u00a0and\u00a0basic\u00a0mathematics\u00a0(GSM8K).\r\n\u25cf\u00a0Search\u00a0engines.\u00a0Information\u00a0Retrieval\u00a0(IR)\u00a0systems\u00a0are\u00a0integral\r\nto \u00a0dialogues, \u00a0question \u00a0answering, \u00a0and \u00a0recommendation \u00a0systems,\r\nserving \u00a0as \u00a0primary \u00a0means \u00a0of \u00a0obtaining \u00a0information. \u00a0LLMs \u00a0can\r\nimprove\u00a0traditional\u00a0IR\u00a0components,\u00a0such\u00a0as\u00a0query\u00a0rewriters,\u00a0and\u00a0can\r\nalso\u00a0function\u00a0as\u00a0the\u00a0engine\u00a0for\u00a0generative\u00a0retrieval.\r\n(i) \u00a0LLM-based \u00a0query \u00a0rewriter. \u00a0The \u00a0query \u00a0rewriter \u00a0enhances \u00a0user\r\nqueries\u00a0by\u00a0adding\u00a0synonyms\u00a0or\u00a0related\u00a0terms\u00a0to\u00a0address\u00a0vocabulary\r\nmismatches \u00a0and \u00a0clarify \u00a0ambiguities, \u00a0thus \u00a0aligning \u00a0more \u00a0accurately\r\nwith \u00a0user \u00a0intent. \u00a0In \u00a0conversational \u00a0retrieval, \u00a0the \u00a0query \u00a0rewriter\r\ncomprehends \u00a0the \u00a0context \u00a0of \u00a0the \u00a0entire \u00a0conversation, \u00a0clarifying\r\nambiguous\u00a0content\u00a0and\u00a0generating\u00a0a\u00a0more\u00a0effective\u00a0new\u00a0query\u00a0based\r\nYao-Yang\u00a0LIU\u00a0et\u00a0al.\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0A\u00a0comprehensive\u00a0taxonomy\u00a0of\u00a0prompt\u00a0engineering\u00a0techniques\u00a0for\u00a0large\u00a0language\u00a0models\r\nFrontiers of Computer Science\u00a0\u00a0|\u00a0Issue\u00a03\u00a0|\u00a0Volume\u00a020\u00a0|\u00a0March\u00a02026\u00a0|\u00a02003601-12\non\u00a0the\u00a0user\u2019s\u00a0dialogue\u00a0history.\r\nHyDE \u00a0[163] \u00a0represents \u00a0pioneering \u00a0work \u00a0on \u00a0LLM-based \u00a0query\r\nrewriting,\u00a0guiding\u00a0LLM\u00a0generation\u00a0using\u00a0various\u00a0prompt\u00a0engineering\r\ntechniques \u00a0in \u00a0Profile \u00a0and \u00a0Perception \u00a0(Subsection \u00a03.1). \u00a0HyDE\r\ngenerates\u00a0detailed\u00a0hypothetical\u00a0documents\u00a0based\u00a0on\u00a0the\u00a0given\u00a0query,\r\nwhich \u00a0are \u00a0then \u00a0retrieved \u00a0from \u00a0the \u00a0corpus \u00a0using \u00a0a \u00a0dense \u00a0retriever.\r\nQuery2doc \u00a0[24,164] \u00a0exemplifies \u00a0another \u00a0innovative \u00a0approach \u00a0to\r\nquery \u00a0rewriting, \u00a0generating \u00a0pseudo-documents \u00a0by \u00a0prompting \u00a0LLMs\r\nwith \u00a0a \u00a0few \u00a0demonstrations, \u00a0reflecting \u00a0the \u00a0use \u00a0of \u00a0the \u00a0Demonstration\r\nInformation\u00a0approach\u00a0(Subsection\u00a03.1).\u00a0These\u00a0pseudo-documents\u00a0are\r\nsubsequently\u00a0expanded\u00a0with\u00a0generated\u00a0documents.\u00a0Based\u00a0on\u00a0prompt\r\nengineering\u00a0optimization,\u00a0Jagerman\u00a0et\u00a0al.\u00a0[165]\u00a0studied\u00a0the\u00a0impact\u00a0of\r\ndifferent \u00a0prompting \u00a0methods \u00a0and \u00a0model \u00a0sizes \u00a0on \u00a0query \u00a0rewriting\r\n[165].\r\nGFF\u00a0[166]\u00a0adopts\u00a0a\u00a0 \u201cgenerate,\u00a0filter,\u00a0and\u00a0fuse\u201d\u00a0method\u00a0for\u00a0query\r\nexpansion, \u00a0utilizing \u00a0LLMs \u00a0to \u00a0extract \u00a0related \u00a0keywords \u00a0from \u00a0the\r\noriginal \u00a0query \u00a0through \u00a0a \u00a0reasoning \u00a0chain. \u00a0GFF \u00a0employs \u00a0prompt\r\nensembling \u00a0strategies \u00a0(Subsection \u00a03.4) \u00a0to \u00a0filter \u00a0generated \u00a0keywords\r\nusing\u00a0techniques\u00a0such\u00a0as\u00a0Self-Consistency\u00a0[143],\u00a0ensuring\u00a0the\u00a0quality\r\nand \u00a0relevance \u00a0of \u00a0keywords, \u00a0which \u00a0are \u00a0then \u00a0integrated \u00a0with \u00a0the\r\noriginal\u00a0query\u00a0for\u00a0downstream\u00a0reranking\u00a0tasks.\r\n(ii) \u00a0LLM-based \u00a0generative \u00a0retrieval. \u00a0Generative \u00a0retrieval \u00a0methods\r\nutilize \u00a0a \u00a0unified \u00a0model \u00a0to \u00a0directly \u00a0generate \u00a0document \u00a0identifiers\r\n(DocIDs) \u00a0related \u00a0to \u00a0user \u00a0queries, \u00a0integrating \u00a0prompt \u00a0engineering\r\ntechniques. \u00a0Traditional \u00a0IR \u00a0systems \u00a0typically \u00a0follow \u00a0the\u00a0 \u201cindex\u0002retrieve-rerank\u201d\u00a0 paradigm, \u00a0which \u00a0has \u00a0proven \u00a0effective \u00a0in \u00a0practice\r\n[163,167]. \u00a0However, \u00a0the \u00a0constituent \u00a0modules \u2014indexing, \u00a0retrieval,\r\nand \u00a0reranking \u2014operate \u00a0independently. \u00a0LLM-based \u00a0generative\r\nretrieval \u00a0unifies \u00a0these \u00a0modules, \u00a0initiating \u00a0a \u00a0new \u00a0paradigm \u00a0for \u00a0IR\r\nsystems.\r\nResearchers\u00a0have\u00a0demonstrated\u00a0that\u00a0LLMs,\u00a0such\u00a0as\u00a0the\u00a0GPT\u00a0series,\r\ncan \u00a0directly \u00a0generate \u00a0URLs \u00a0related \u00a0to \u00a0user \u00a0queries \u00a0[168]. \u00a0This\r\ncapability \u00a0allows \u00a0the \u00a0LLM \u00a0to \u00a0function \u00a0as \u00a0a \u00a0generative \u00a0retriever,\r\nproducing \u00a0document \u00a0identifiers \u00a0from \u00a0the \u00a0original \u00a0input \u00a0to \u00a0obtain\r\nrelevant \u00a0documents. \u00a0Ziems \u00a0et \u00a0al. \u00a0[168] \u00a0introduced \u00a0the \u00a0LLM-URL\r\nmodel,\u00a0which\u00a0employs\u00a0the\u00a0GPT-3\u00a0text-davinci-003\u00a0model\u00a0to\u00a0generate\r\ncandidate\u00a0URLs.\u00a0It\u00a0utilizes\u00a0the\u00a0Demonstration\u00a0Information\u00a0approach\r\n(Section \u00a03.1) \u00a0to \u00a0standardize \u00a0model \u00a0output \u00a0and \u00a0incorporates \u00a0a \u00a0URL\r\nfiltering\u00a0mechanism\u00a0that\u00a0extracts\u00a0valid\u00a0URLs\u00a0from\u00a0candidates\u00a0using\r\nregular\u00a0expressions.\r\n\u25cf \u00a0Professional \u00a0knowledge \u00a0Q&A. \u00a0The \u00a0expansive \u00a0capabilities \u00a0of\r\nLLMs\u00a0enable\u00a0them\u00a0to\u00a0possess\u00a0specialized\u00a0knowledge\u00a0across\u00a0various\r\nfields, \u00a0effectively \u00a0organizing \u00a0and \u00a0presenting \u00a0information \u00a0to \u00a0address\r\nspecific\u00a0inquiries.\u00a0This\u00a0ability\u00a0to\u00a0provide\u00a0accurate\u00a0responses\u00a0to\u00a0user\r\nqueries\u00a0is\u00a0commonly\u00a0referred\u00a0to\u00a0as\u00a0professional\u00a0question\u00a0and\u00a0answer\r\n(QA).\r\nLawGPT \u00a0[169] \u00a0is \u00a0a \u00a0robust \u00a0language \u00a0model \u00a0designed \u00a0to \u00a0address\r\nlegal \u00a0knowledge \u00a0inquiries \u00a0with \u00a0high \u00a0accuracy. \u00a0It \u00a0employs \u00a0the \u00a0LLM\r\ninternal\u00a0feedback\u00a0method\u00a0(Subsection\u00a03.3)\u00a0to\u00a0continually\u00a0enhance\u00a0its\r\nprecision \u00a0in \u00a0legal \u00a0question \u00a0answering. \u00a0Through \u00a0this \u00a0approach,\r\nLawGPT\u00a0generates\u00a0legal\u00a0queries\u00a0pertinent\u00a0to\u00a0specific\u00a0legal\u00a0texts\u00a0and\r\nsubsequently \u00a0provides \u00a0responses \u00a0in \u00a0the \u00a0form \u00a0of\u00a0 \u201ctext \u00a0segment\u0002question\u201d\u00a0 pairs, \u00a0ensuring \u00a0that \u00a0its \u00a0answers \u00a0are \u00a0rich \u00a0in \u00a0legal\r\ninformation.\r\nMultiMedQA \u00a0[170] \u00a0is \u00a0a \u00a0benchmark \u00a0that \u00a0integrates \u00a0clinical\r\nexpertise\u00a0with\u00a0medical\u00a0knowledge,\u00a0employing\u00a0a\u00a0Few-shot\u00a0prompting\r\ntechnique \u00a0(Subsection \u00a03.1). \u00a0Collaborating \u00a0closely \u00a0with \u00a0a \u00a0panel \u00a0of\r\nseasoned \u00a0clinicians, \u00a0MultiMedQA \u00a0produces \u00a0exemplary \u00a0few-shot\r\ndemonstrations \u00a0and \u00a0sample \u00a0scenarios. \u00a0Moreover, \u00a0it \u00a0adeptly\r\ndemonstrates \u00a0Reasoning \u00a0and \u00a0Planning \u00a0capabilities, \u00a0exhibiting \u00a0a\r\nrobust \u00a0chain-of-thought \u00a0process \u00a0(Subsection \u00a03.3) \u00a0for \u00a0a \u00a0myriad \u00a0of\r\nmedical \u00a0issues \u00a0by \u00a0leveraging \u00a0insights \u00a0from \u00a0various \u00a0medical\r\nprofessionals.\u00a0Furthermore,\u00a0MultiMedQA\u00a0excels\u00a0in\u00a0internal\u00a0feedback\r\n(Subsection\u00a03.3)\u00a0verification,\u00a0a\u00a0crucial\u00a0aspect\u00a0in\u00a0refining\u00a0its\u00a0accuracy.\r\nGiven\u00a0the\u00a0multifaceted\u00a0nature\u00a0of\u00a0medical\u00a0queries,\u00a0it\u00a0employs\u00a0the\u00a0self\u0002consistency\u00a0strategy\u00a0(Subsection\u00a03.4),\u00a0allowing\u00a0the\u00a0model\u00a0to\u00a0compare\r\nand\u00a0evaluate\u00a0diverse\u00a0perspectives\u00a0to\u00a0ensure\u00a0coherence\u00a0and\u00a0reliability\r\nin\u00a0its\u00a0responses.\r\n\u25cf \u00a0Training \u00a0data \u00a0augmentation. \u00a0Due \u00a0to \u00a0the \u00a0high \u00a0cost \u00a0of \u00a0manually\r\nannotating \u00a0labels, \u00a0a \u00a0common \u00a0challenge \u00a0in \u00a0training \u00a0neural \u00a0retrieval\r\nmodels \u00a0is \u00a0the \u00a0lack \u00a0of \u00a0training \u00a0data. \u00a0LLMs \u00a0can \u00a0learn \u00a0patterns \u00a0from\r\nmanually\u00a0annotated\u00a0data\u00a0and\u00a0generate\u00a0additional\u00a0data\u00a0consistent\u00a0with\r\nthe\u00a0existing\u00a0dataset.\r\nYoo \u00a0et \u00a0al. \u00a0[171] \u00a0proposed \u00a0GPT3Mix, \u00a0which \u00a0generates \u00a0synthetic\r\ndata \u00a0from \u00a0existing \u00a0datasets \u00a0based \u00a0on \u00a0the \u00a0GPT3 \u00a0LLM. \u00a0GPT3Mix\r\nemploys\u00a0the\u00a0Demonstration\u00a0Information\u00a0method\u00a0(Subsection\u00a03.1)\u00a0and\r\nthe \u00a0Task \u00a0Information \u00a0method \u00a0(Subsection \u00a03.1). \u00a0The \u00a0prompts \u00a0of\r\nGPT3Mix\u00a0include\u00a0two\u00a0parts:\u00a0real\u00a0examples\u00a0from\u00a0the\u00a0dataset\u00a0and\u00a0task\r\nspecifications, \u00a0which \u00a0are \u00a0used \u00a0to \u00a0create \u00a0synthetic \u00a0data \u00a0and \u00a0pseudo\r\nlabels.\r\nYoo \u00a0et \u00a0al. \u00a0[171] \u00a0utilized \u00a0this \u00a0new \u00a0augmented \u00a0dataset \u00a0to \u00a0fine-tune\r\nBERT \u00a0and \u00a0DistilBERT \u00a0models, \u00a0achieving \u00a0excellent \u00a0performance \u00a0in\r\nclassification\u00a0tasks.\u00a0In\u00a0the\u00a0context\u00a0of\u00a0information\u00a0retrieval,\u00a0it\u00a0is\u00a0easy\r\nto\u00a0collect\u00a0many\u00a0documents;\u00a0however,\u00a0the\u00a0challenging\u00a0and\u00a0expensive\r\ntask\u00a0is\u00a0to\u00a0collect\u00a0real\u00a0user\u00a0queries\u00a0and\u00a0label\u00a0the\u00a0relevant\u00a0documents\r\naccordingly.\u00a0Given\u00a0the\u00a0LLM\u2019s\u00a0powerful\u00a0natural\u00a0language\u00a0processing\r\ncapabilities, \u00a0many \u00a0researchers \u00a0[172,173] \u00a0suggested \u00a0using \u00a0an \u00a0LLM\u0002driven\u00a0process\u00a0to\u00a0create\u00a0pseudo\u00a0queries\u00a0or\u00a0relevance\u00a0labels\u00a0based\u00a0on\r\nexisting\u00a0datasets.\r\nIn\u00a0cutting-edge\u00a0work,\u00a0Dai\u00a0et\u00a0al.\u00a0[174]\u00a0introduced\u00a0ChatAug,\u00a0which\r\ntransforms \u00a0training \u00a0samples \u00a0from \u00a0a \u00a0small \u00a0dataset \u00a0into \u00a0multiple\r\nsamples \u00a0that \u00a0are \u00a0conceptually \u00a0similar \u00a0but \u00a0semantically \u00a0distinct.\r\nChatAug \u00a0outperforms \u00a0state-of-the-art \u00a0text \u00a0data \u00a0augmentation\r\nmethods \u00a0in \u00a0terms \u00a0of \u00a0test \u00a0accuracy \u00a0and \u00a0augmented \u00a0sample\r\ndistribution.\r\n2)\u00a0In-depth\u00a0information\u00a0analysis\r\nIn \u00a0addition \u00a0to \u00a0providing \u00a0information, \u00a0LLMs \u00a0can \u00a0leverage \u00a0their\r\nreasoning \u00a0capabilities \u00a0to \u00a0analyze \u00a0patterns \u00a0within \u00a0specific \u00a0data \u00a0or\r\ninformation. \u00a0Applications \u00a0requiring \u00a0the \u00a0evaluation \u00a0of \u00a0complex\r\nsystems\u00a0are\u00a0categorized\u00a0under\u00a0In-depth\u00a0Information\u00a0Analysis.\r\nFront.\u00a0Comput.\u00a0Sci.,\u00a02026,\u00a020(3):\u00a02003601\r\nFrontiers of Computer Science\u00a0\u00a0|\u00a0Issue\u00a03\u00a0|\u00a0Volume\u00a020\u00a0|\u00a0March\u00a02026\u00a0|\u00a02003601-13\n\u25cf \u00a0Financial \u00a0markets. \u00a0By \u00a0providing \u00a0Internet-scale \u00a0data \u00a0for \u00a0LLMs,\r\nthese \u00a0models \u00a0can \u00a0utilize \u00a0hybrid \u00a0training \u00a0methods \u00a0in \u00a0financial \u00a0tasks,\r\ndriving \u00a0open-source \u00a0development \u00a0in \u00a0the \u00a0financial \u00a0field.\r\nBloombergGPT \u00a0[175] \u00a0is \u00a0a \u00a0formidable \u00a0large \u00a0language \u00a0model \u00a0with \u00a05\r\nbillion\u00a0parameters,\u00a0meticulously\u00a0trained\u00a0to\u00a0excel\u00a0in\u00a0the\u00a0intricate\u00a0realm\r\nof\u00a0finance\u00a0through\u00a0vast\u00a0datasets.\r\nBloombergGPT\u00a0combines\u00a0prompt\u00a0engineering\u00a0technologies\u00a0such\u00a0as\r\npersonality\u00a0information\u00a0(Subsection\u00a03.1)\u00a0and\u00a0external\u00a0financial\u00a0tools\r\n(Subsection \u00a03.3) \u00a0to \u00a0provide \u00a0personalized, \u00a0time-sensitive \u00a0financial\r\nadvice.\u00a0Its\u00a0versatility\u00a0extends\u00a0across\u00a0various\u00a0tasks\u00a0within\u00a0the\u00a0financial\r\nsector,\u00a0making\u00a0it\u00a0beneficial\u00a0for\u00a0professionals.\u00a0Leveraging\u00a0techniques\r\nsuch \u00a0as \u00a0few-shot \u00a0learning \u00a0and \u00a0other \u00a0sophisticated \u00a0methodologies,\r\nscholars \u00a0fine-tune \u00a0BloombergGPT \u00a0to \u00a0suit \u00a0specific \u00a0task \u00a0formats,\r\nthereby\u00a0enhancing\u00a0its\u00a0efficacy\u00a0in\u00a0delivering\u00a0best-in-class\u00a0results.\r\nFinGPT\u00a0[176]\u00a0stands\u00a0out\u00a0as\u00a0an\u00a0open-source,\u00a0large\u00a0language\u00a0model\r\ntailored \u00a0specifically \u00a0for \u00a0the \u00a0financial \u00a0sector, \u00a0boasting \u00a0versatile\r\napplications\u00a0such\u00a0as\u00a0robot\u00a0consultation,\u00a0algorithmic\u00a0trading,\u00a0and\u00a0low\u0002code \u00a0accessibility. \u00a0Its \u00a0remarkable \u00a0capability \u00a0lies \u00a0in \u00a0making\r\nquantitative \u00a0inferences \u00a0from \u00a0vast \u00a0financial \u00a0datasets, \u00a0effectively\r\ncapturing \u00a0the \u00a0intricate \u00a0dynamics \u00a0of \u00a0the \u00a0financial \u00a0markets. \u00a0A \u00a0key\r\nfeature \u00a0of \u00a0FinGPT \u00a0is \u00a0its \u00a0adept \u00a0utilization \u00a0of \u00a0external \u00a0feedback\r\nmethods\u00a0(Subsection\u00a03.3)\u00a0within\u00a0prompt\u00a0engineering.\u00a0By\u00a0leveraging\r\nstock\u00a0prices\u00a0as\u00a0indicators,\u00a0FinGPT\u00a0engages\u00a0in\u00a0reinforcement\u00a0learning,\r\ncontinuously\u00a0refining\u00a0its\u00a0understanding\u00a0and\u00a0interpretation\u00a0of\u00a0financial\r\ntexts. \u00a0This \u00a0process \u00a0empowers \u00a0FinGPT \u00a0to \u00a0anticipate \u00a0and \u00a0predict\r\nmarket \u00a0responses \u00a0to \u00a0a \u00a0wide \u00a0array \u00a0of \u00a0financial \u00a0events, \u00a0thereby\r\nenhancing\u00a0its\u00a0overall\u00a0performance\u00a0and\u00a0utility\u00a0in\u00a0financial\u00a0analysis\u00a0and\r\ndecision-making.\r\n\u25cf \u00a0Chemical \u00a0molecules. \u00a0The \u00a0study \u00a0of \u00a0chemical \u00a0molecules\r\nencompasses \u00a0the \u00a0properties, \u00a0composition, \u00a0structure, \u00a0and \u00a0chemical\r\nreactions \u00a0of \u00a0matter. \u00a0This \u00a0field \u00a0involves \u00a0complex \u00a0computational \u00a0and\r\npredictive \u00a0tasks, \u00a0such \u00a0as \u00a0property \u00a0prediction, \u00a0chemical \u00a0structure\r\noptimization, \u00a0and \u00a0reaction \u00a0prediction. \u00a0As \u00a0data \u00a0scales \u00a0increase,\r\ntraditional\u00a0chemical\u00a0computational\u00a0methods\u00a0can\u00a0no\u00a0longer\u00a0meet\u00a0the\r\ndemand,\u00a0making\u00a0the\u00a0application\u00a0of\u00a0LLMs\u00a0in\u00a0chemistry\u00a0increasingly\r\nimportant.\r\nBioinspiredLLM \u00a0[177] \u00a0is \u00a0an \u00a0autoregressive \u00a0transformation \u00a0large\r\nlanguage\u00a0model\u00a0specifically\u00a0tailored\u00a0for\u00a0biomaterials\u00a0and\u00a0biomimetic\r\nmaterials.\u00a0This\u00a0sophisticated\u00a0model\u00a0excels\u00a0in\u00a0accurately\u00a0recalling\u00a0vast\r\namounts \u00a0of \u00a0information \u00a0pertaining \u00a0to \u00a0biomaterials, \u00a0effectively\r\nreflecting \u00a0intricate \u00a0patterns \u00a0between \u00a0various \u00a0biomaterials, \u00a0and\r\nfacilitating \u00a0research \u00a0tasks \u00a0within \u00a0this \u00a0field. \u00a0Scientific \u00a0researchers\r\ncontinuously \u00a0uncover \u00a0new \u00a0patterns, \u00a0and \u00a0BioinspiredLLM\r\naccommodates \u00a0this \u00a0by \u00a0offering \u00a0additional \u00a0contextual \u00a0content \u00a0when\r\nqueried. \u00a0Moreover, \u00a0the \u00a0model \u00a0leverages \u00a0the \u00a0Retrieve \u00a0and \u00a0Generate\r\n(RAG) \u00a0framework, \u00a0based \u00a0on \u00a0Knowledge \u00a0prompt \u00a0engineering\r\ntechniques\u00a0(Subsection\u00a03.2),\u00a0to\u00a0provide\u00a0comprehensive\u00a0and\u00a0insightful\r\nanswers.\r\nChatDrug \u00a0[178] \u00a0harnesses \u00a0conversational \u00a0and \u00a0reasoning\r\ncapabilities \u00a0to \u00a0facilitate \u00a0AI-assisted \u00a0drug \u00a0discovery \u00a0endeavors.\r\nChatDrug\u00a0employs\u00a0Chain-of-Thought\u00a0(CoT)\u00a0technology\u00a0(Subsection\r\n3.3) \u00a0to \u00a0decompose \u00a0complex \u00a0concepts \u00a0into \u00a0more \u00a0understandable\r\nattributes, \u00a0thereby \u00a0improving \u00a0reasoning \u00a0ability \u00a0and \u00a0problem-solving\r\nefficiency. \u00a0Additionally, \u00a0ChatDrug \u00a0incorporates \u00a0prompt \u00a0design\r\ntailored \u00a0for \u00a0domain-specific \u00a0modules, \u00a0with \u00a0the \u00a0flexibility \u00a0to\r\nimplement \u00a0prompt \u00a0functions \u00a0via \u00a0few-shot \u00a0learning \u00a0methodologies\r\n(Subsection \u00a03.1). \u00a0Leveraging \u00a0the \u00a0Retrieve \u00a0and \u00a0Generate \u00a0(RAG)\r\nmethod \u00a0(Subsection \u00a03.2) \u00a0enriches \u00a0ChatDrug\u2019s \u00a0professional\r\nknowledge,\u00a0thereby\u00a0enhancing\u00a0the\u00a0quality\u00a0of\u00a0responses.\r\nChemCrow \u00a0[179] \u00a0enables \u00a0reasoning \u00a0across \u00a0common \u00a0chemistry\r\ntasks \u00a0such \u00a0as \u00a0material \u00a0design \u00a0and \u00a0synthesis, \u00a0from \u00a0reasoning \u00a0about\r\nsimple\u00a0drug\u00a0discovery\u00a0cycles\u00a0to\u00a0planning\u00a0the\u00a0synthesis\u00a0of\u00a0substances\r\nacross\u00a0a\u00a0wide\u00a0range\u00a0of\u00a0molecular\u00a0complexity.\u00a0ChemCrow\u00a0combines\r\nthe \u00a0inferential \u00a0power \u00a0of \u00a0LLMs \u00a0with \u00a0the \u00a0chemistry \u00a0expertise \u00a0of\r\ncomputational \u00a0tools \u00a0(Subsection \u00a03.2), \u00a0successfully \u00a0planning \u00a0and\r\nsynthesizing \u00a0an \u00a0insect \u00a0repellent, \u00a0three \u00a0organocatalysts, \u00a0and \u00a0guiding\r\nthe \u00a0screening \u00a0and \u00a0synthesis \u00a0of \u00a0a \u00a0novel \u00a0chromophore \u00a0with \u00a0target\r\nproperties. \u00a0Enhanced \u00a0by \u00a0the \u00a0RAG \u00a0method \u00a0(Subsection \u00a03.2) \u00a0and\r\nsearch\u00a0engine\u00a0tools\u00a0(Subsection\u00a03.3),\u00a0ChemCrow\u00a0can\u00a0obtain\u00a0scientific\r\ninformation\u00a0from\u00a0the\u00a0Internet\u00a0and\u00a0build\u00a0relevant\u00a0databases.\u00a0It\u00a0can\u00a0also\r\naccept\u00a0external\u00a0feedback\u00a0from\u00a0humans\u00a0and\u00a0adjust\u00a0itself\u00a0accordingly.\r\n4.2\u00a0\u00a0Transformative\u00a0applications\u00a0of\u00a0LLMs\r\nTransformative \u00a0applications \u00a0of \u00a0LLMs \u00a0facilitate \u00a0automation \u00a0and\r\nenhance \u00a0workflows \u00a0traditionally \u00a0dependent \u00a0on \u00a0human \u00a0input. \u00a0These\r\napplications \u00a0can \u00a0be \u00a0broadly \u00a0categorized \u00a0into \u00a0physical \u00a0world\r\napplications\u00a0and\u00a0creative\u00a0applications.\u00a0Through\u00a0prompt\u00a0engineering,\r\nLLMs \u00a0can \u00a0impact \u00a0the \u00a0physical \u00a0world \u00a0across \u00a0various \u00a0application\r\nscenarios,\u00a0including\u00a0software\u00a0engineering,\u00a0robotics,\u00a0and\u00a0expert-level\r\ntask \u00a0automation. \u00a0Conversely, \u00a0the \u00a0impact \u00a0of \u00a0LLMs \u00a0on \u00a0creative\r\ndomains\u00a0extends\u00a0to\u00a0areas\u00a0traditionally\u00a0reserved\u00a0for\u00a0human\u00a0creativity\r\nand\u00a0artistic\u00a0expression,\u00a0including\u00a0language\u00a0generation,\u00a0visual\u00a0content\r\ncreation,\u00a0and\u00a0auditory\u00a0processing.\u00a0These\u00a0enhancements\u00a0contribute\u00a0to\r\nexpanding\u00a0human\u00a0creativity\u00a0and\u00a0comprehension.\r\n1)\u00a0Physical\u00a0world\u00a0applications\r\nApplications\u00a0of\u00a0LLMs\u00a0in\u00a0the\u00a0physical\u00a0world\u00a0encompass\u00a0areas\u00a0such\u00a0as\r\nsoftware\u00a0engineering,\u00a0robotics,\u00a0and\u00a0advanced\u00a0automation.\r\n\u25cf \u00a0Software \u00a0engineering. \u00a0One \u00a0of \u00a0the \u00a0most \u00a0advanced \u00a0and \u00a0widely\r\nused \u00a0applications \u00a0of \u00a0LLMs \u00a0is \u00a0generating \u00a0and \u00a0completing \u00a0computer\r\nprograms\u00a0in\u00a0various\u00a0programming\u00a0languages.\u00a0This\u00a0section\u00a0discusses\r\nprogramming-specific \u00a0LLMs, \u00a0which \u00a0are \u00a0fine-tuned \u00a0or \u00a0pre-trained\r\nspecifically\u00a0for\u00a0programming\u00a0applications.\u00a0However,\u00a0it\u00a0is\u00a0important\r\nto \u00a0note \u00a0that \u00a0general \u00a0chatbots, \u00a0which \u00a0are \u00a0partially \u00a0trained \u00a0on \u00a0code\r\ndatasets\u00a0(such\u00a0as\u00a0ChatGPT),\u00a0are\u00a0increasingly\u00a0utilized\u00a0in\u00a0programming\r\ntasks.\r\nCode \u00a0generation \u00a0refers \u00a0to \u00a0the \u00a0use \u00a0of \u00a0LLMs \u00a0to \u00a0output \u00a0new \u00a0code\r\nbased \u00a0on \u00a0the \u00a0requirements \u00a0provided \u00a0in \u00a0the \u00a0prompts. \u00a0Several \u00a0LLMs\r\nand \u00a0methods \u00a0have \u00a0been \u00a0proposed \u00a0for \u00a0computer \u00a0programming.\r\nOpenAI\u00a0first\u00a0released\u00a0CodeX\u00a0[50],\u00a0an\u00a0LLM\u00a0based\u00a0on\u00a0GPT-3\u00a0(up\u00a0to\r\nYao-Yang\u00a0LIU\u00a0et\u00a0al.\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0A\u00a0comprehensive\u00a0taxonomy\u00a0of\u00a0prompt\u00a0engineering\u00a0techniques\u00a0for\u00a0large\u00a0language\u00a0models\r\nFrontiers of Computer Science\u00a0\u00a0|\u00a0Issue\u00a03\u00a0|\u00a0Volume\u00a020\u00a0|\u00a0March\u00a02026\u00a0|\u00a02003601-14\n12B \u00a0parameters) \u00a0pre-trained \u00a0on \u00a0public \u00a0This \u00a0dual \u00a0role\r\nintroduces\u00a0risks,\u00a0as\u00a0specific\u00a0prompts\u00a0can\u00a0be\u00a0crafted\u00a0to\u00a0induce\u00a0harmful\r\noutputs \u00a0from \u00a0LLMs, \u00a0a \u00a0prevent \u00a0generating \u00a0risky \u00a0responses. \u00a0Profile \u00a0and \u00a0instruction, \u00a0in\r\nSubsection \u00a03.1, \u00a0may \u00a0be \u00a0useful \u00a0in \u00a0such \u00a0reasoning \u00a0techniques, \u00a0such \u00a0as\r\nfeedback\u00a0mechanisms\u00a0[184],\u00a0could\u00a0improve\u00a0the\u00a0cognitive\u00a0efficacy\u00a0of\r\nRAG, \u00a0facilitating \u00a0its \u00a0application \u00a0in \u00a0a \u00a0more \u00a0contextually \u00a0appropriate\r\nmanner. \u00a0Current \u00a0methods \u00a0[184,185] \u00a0predominantly \u00a0rely \u00a0on Typically, personality information covers key \u00b7 characteristics like age, gender, and profession [20], along with tone \u00b7 and psychological traits, thereby reflecting the personality of the \u00b7 LLM\u2019s role. Temperature 0.2, nucleus p 0.95, max tokens 512, frequency penalty 0, presence penalty 0.\n\nLarge language models have achieved impressive results across various tasks but remain limited in their ability to adapt ethically and structurally across diverse domains without retraining. This paper presents the Inclusive Prompt Engineering Model (IPEM), a modular framework designed to enhance LLM performance, adaptability, and ethical alignment through prompt-level strategies alone. IPEM integrates four components: Memory-of-Thought for multi-turn consistency, Enhanced Chain-of-Thought prompting for logical verification, Structured and Analogical Reasoning modules for tabular and cross-domain tasks, and Evaluation and Feedback Loops that incorporate uncertainty-aware selection and bias mitigation mechanisms. Evaluated across tasks in arithmetic reasoning, healthcare triage, financial forecasting, and inclusive question answering, IPEM consistently improves model outputs over a GPT-4 baseline.\n\nArtificial Intelligence Review - Large language models have achieved impressive results across various tasks but remain limited in their ability to adapt ethically and structurally across diverse...\n\nAll experiments used the OpenAI GPT-4_1-2025\u201304-14 checkpoint accessed through the API. For both of them, the system prompt plays a huge role.\n\nThis is the [system prompt](https://gist.github.com/cablej/ccfe7fe097d8bbb05519bacfeb910038) for [Cluely](https://app.cluely.com/login):\n\n[![](https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!r0bv!,w_1456,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2F0e9ca35f-9f8d-42d5-bf33-9197fcc1e7a5_1366x714.png)](https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!r0bv!,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2F0e9ca35f-9f8d-42d5-bf33-9197fcc1e7a5_1366x714.png)\n\nIt\u2019s a longer prompt but we\u2019re focusing on the beginning.\n\nThere\u2019s a lot of interesting things to notice here:\n\n1. The use of brackets, like code\n2. Never and always lists\n3. Display instructions\n4. If/then edge cases\n\nThis prompt, plus Cluely\u2019s liquid glass UX, is doing a lot of the heavy lifting behind reaching $6M ARR in just 2 months.\n\nThis is the [system prompt](https://github.com/stackblitz/bolt.new/blob/main/app/lib/.server/llm/prompts.ts) for [Bolt](https://bolt.new/):\n\n[![](https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!WOW_!,w_1456,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2Ff43fec3a-e7ef-4f59-92e0-7fa5ea47f493_1368x1596.png)](https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!WOW_!,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2Ff43fec3a-e7ef-4f59-92e0-7fa5ea47f493_1368x1596.png)\n\nThere\u2019s a lot of repeated patterns from Cluely, like code formatting and long lists of what to do with all caps.\n\nThere\u2019s also some Bolt specific stuff like extremely detailed handling of errors they likely faced in the past testing the product.\n\nAman Khan (Director of AI PM at Arize) went so far as [to say](https://youtu.be/Ej4pBDaHspk?si=YAvHO6EgCBu_BLef&t=5555) that **this is one of the keys to Bolt\u2019s success**. They likely wouldn\u2019t have achieved **$50M ARR in 5 months** without such a powerful prompt.\n\nThe point being: **great prompt engineering can be the difference between AI product success and failure**.\n\n[Share](https://www.news.aakashg.com/p/prompt-engineering?utm_source=substack&utm_medium=email&utm_content=share&action=share)\n\n---\n\n### Prompt Engineering is a Key Part of Context Engineering\n\nPeople will say: \u201c*the new hotness is context engineering*!\u201d And they\u2019re right: it is!\n\n[![](https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!2zvY!,w_1456,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2F423f7be9-fd4d-4314-afb8-0a1797fcd156_1302x1362.png)](https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!2zvY!,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2F423f7be9-fd4d-4314-afb8-0a1797fcd156_1302x1362.png)\n\nI went in-depth into [context engineering](https://www.news.aakashg.com/p/rag-vs-fine-tuning-vs-prompt-engineering) last week. One of the key takeaways? P**rompt engineering is almost always a part of the picture.**\n\nAnd in many cases, it can do 85% of the heavy lifting.\n\n---\n\n### Key PM Skill\n\nSo - welcome to 2025, **where every PM needs to be good at prompt engineering**.\n\nIt\u2019s **not something you can just outsource** to engineering. You want to be an *active contributor* to the process. *There\u2019s at least 4 reasons*.\n\n[![](https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!1LH4!,w_1456,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2F4871cae5-d024-4d0c-a951-2f923a732fe1_3600x4500.png)](https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!1LH4!,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2F4871cae5-d024-4d0c-a951-2f923a732fe1_3600x4500.png)\n\n1. PMs understand user intent better than anyone\n2. When you can modify prompts yourself rather than waiting for engineering cycles, you can iterate faster\n3. Prompt engineering is product strategy in disguise **-** every instruction you write into a system prompt is a product decision\n4. You'll spot opportunities others miss **-** you'll recognize when a user complaint isn't actually a model limitation, it's a prompt engineering opportunity\n\nIn fact, when I shipped the AI e-mail writer at Apollo.io, I was *regularly* working with the team to iterate on the prompts. I learned it\u2019s not just **necessary** - it\u2019s **exciting**.\n\nThe best AI PMs are using the AI wave to get more into the technical implementation: and **I encourage you to as well**! It\u2019s an opportunity to get closer to the \u201cbare metal.\u201d\n\n*So, for all these reasons, I figured the PMs of the world needed an **authoritative** guide to prompt engineering.*\n\n---\n\n## Today\u2019s Deep Dive\n\n*We\u2019ve put together the most up-to-date and practical guide on prompt engineering out there:*\n\n1. **Do You Really Need Prompt Engineering?**\n2. **The Hidden Economics of Prompt Engineering**\n3. **What the Research Says About Good Prompts**\n4. **The 6-Layer Bottom-Line Framework**\n5. **Step-by-step: Improving Your Prompts as a PM**\n6. **The 201+301 Advanced Techniques Nobody Talks About**\n7. **The Ultimate Prompt Template 2.0**\n8. **The 3 Most Common Mistakes**\n\n*It\u2019s the wisdom we\u2019ve collected shipping AI at places like OpenAI, Shopify, & Google.*\n\nSubscribe\n\n---\n\n## 1. Do You Really Need Prompt Engineering?\n\nBefore we go any further, do you really need prompt engineering?\n\nIt depends on *the state of your current prompt* and *where you are in productionizing it*.\n\nHere\u2019s a **simple playbook** to figure out where you are and where you need to go:\n\n[Get the Playbook](https://docs.google.com/document/d/1pormS3jlw8J2ETvAvUDdw81Wl1BPF3Kk6alt8npcRvY/edit?tab=t.0)\n\n*Now that you know whether prompt engineering is worth your time, let's dive into how the best teams actually do it.*\n\n---\n\n## 2. The Hidden Economics of Prompt Engineering\n\nWe want to emphasize to you how important this is by first saying: ***it\u2019s not just abut revenue***.\n\nA great prompt can 100x revenue you to a Cluely/Bolt state if you do it right. But prompt engineering also can reduce costs.\n\n### The Real Cost Equation\n\n[![](https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!BgBU!,w_1456,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2F90440199-24b1-4101-870c-936c3a9e72b7_3600x4500.png)](https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!BgBU!,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2F90440199-24b1-4101-870c-936c3a9e72b7_3600x4500.png)\n\nTotal AI Cost = (Input Tokens \\* Price Per Input Token) + (Output Tokens \u00d7 Price per Output Token) \u00d7 Number of Calls\n\nSeems simple. But watch what happens with different prompt strategies:\n\n**Detailed Approach (eg Bolt)**:\n\n* Prompt: 2,500 tokens (detailed instructions)\n* Output: 1500 tokens\n* **Cost per call:** $0.03 *(at $0.003 per 1k input + $0.015 per 1k output for Claude Sonnet 4)*\n* Daily volume: 100,000 calls\n* **Daily cost: $3,000**\n\n**Simpler Approach (eg Cluely)**:\n\n* Prompt: 212 tokens (structured + few-shot)\n* Output: 400 tokens (constrained format)\n* **Cost per call:** $0.00706 *(at $0.005 per 1k input + $0.015 per 1k output for GPT-4o)*\n* Daily volume: 100,000 calls\n* **Daily cost: $706**\n\nThat's a 76% cost reduction.\n\nShorter, structured prompts also:\n\n1. Have less variance in outputs\n2. Come out faster with less latency\n\nSo there\u2019s a lot to be said about prompt engineering on the cost side.\n\n### Short vs Long: How to Decide\n\nShorter prompts and outputs have their benefits in terms of cost. But sometimes that 88% increase in cost is well worth it!\n\nYou have to weigh the performance vs the cost. A very common approach used by the best AI teams these days is the \u201chill climb up quality first\u201d and then \u201cdown climb cost second\u201d:\n\n[![](https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!uclj!,w_1456,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2F9fd53d3e-2bc7-4d59-86af-dbb1cc7623a3_3600x4500.png)](https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!uclj!,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2F9fd53d3e-2bc7-4d59-86af-dbb1cc7623a3_3600x4500.png)\n\nAlong the way, it\u2019s a delicate balancing act of model performance against evals, error analysis, and context engineering (via prompt engineering, RAG, and fine-tuning).\n\n*We\u2019ll walk you through, step-by-step, how to in section 4.*\n\n---\n\n## 3. What the Research Says About Good Prompts\n\nThe cool thing about prompting is that, now that that we have actual research studies on what makes for a good prompt.\n\nWe don\u2019t need to listen to random influencers.         "text": "     1\t---\n     2\tname: xlsx\n     3\tdescription: \"Use this skill any time a spreadsheet file is the primary input or output. This means any task where the user wants to: open, read, edit, or fix an existing .xlsx, .xlsm, .csv, or .tsv file (e.g., adding columns, computing formulas, formatting, charting, cleaning messy data); create a new spreadsheet from scratch or from other data sources; or convert between tabular file formats. Trigger especially when the user references a spreadsheet file by name or path \u2014 even casually (like \\\"the xlsx in my downloads\\\") \u2014 and wants something done to it or produced from it. Also trigger for cleaning or restructuring messy tabular data files (malformed rows, misplaced headers, junk data) into proper spreadsheets. The deliverable must be a spreadsheet file. Do NOT trigger when the primary deliverable is a Word document, HTML report, standalone Python script, database pipeline, or Google Sheets API integration, even if tabular data is involved.\"\n     4\tlicense: Proprietary. LICENSE.txt has complete terms\n     5\t---\n     6\t\n     7\t# Requirements for Outputs\n     8\t\n     9\t## All Excel files\n    10\t\n    11\t### Professional Font\n    12\t- Use a consistent, professional font (e.g., Arial, Times New Roman) for all deliverables unless otherwise instructed by the user\n    13\t\n    14\t### Zero Formula Errors\n    15\t- Every Excel model MUST be delivered with ZERO formula errors (#REF!, #DIV/0!, #VALUE!, #N/A, #NAME?)\n    16\t\n    17\t### Preserve Existing Templates (when updating templates)\n    18\t- Study and EXACTLY match existing format, style, and conventions when modifying files\n    19\t- Never impose standardized formatting on files with established patterns\n    20\t- Existing template conventions ALWAYS override these guidelines\n    21\t\n    22\t## Financial models\n    23\t\n    24\t### Color Coding Standards\n    25\tUnless otherwise stated by the user or existing template\n    26\t\n    27\t#### Industry-Standard Color Conventions\n    28\t- **Blue text (RGB: 0,0,255)**: Hardcoded inputs, and numbers users will change for scenarios\n    29\t- **Black text (RGB: 0,0,0)**: ALL formulas and calculations\n    30\t- **Green text (RGB: 0,128,0)**: Links pulling from other worksheets within same workbook\n    31\t- **Red text (RGB: 255,0,0)**: External links to other files\n    32\t- **Yellow background (RGB: 255,255,0)**: Key assumptions needing attention or cells that need to be updated\n    33\t\n    34\t### Number Formatting Standards\n    35\t\n    36\t#### Required Format Rules\n    37\t- **Years**: Format as text strings (e.g., \"2024\" not \"2,024\")\n    38\t- **Currency**: Use $#,##0 format; ALWAYS specify units in headers (\"Revenue ($mm)\")\n    39\t- **Zeros**: Use number formatting to make all zeros \"-\", including percentages (e.g., \"$#,##0;($#,##0);-\")\n    40\t- **Percentages**: Default to 0.0% format (one decimal)\n    41\t- **Multiples**: Format as 0.0x for valuation multiples (EV/EBITDA, P/E)\n    42\t- **Negative numbers**: Use parentheses (123) not minus -123\n    43\t\n    44\t### Formula Construction Rules\n    45\t\n    46\t#### Assumptions Placement\n    47\t- Place ALL assumptions (growth rates, margins, multiples, etc.) in separate assumption cells\n    48\t- Use cell references instead of hardcoded values in formulas\n    49\t- Example: Use =B5*(1+$B$6) instead of =B5*1.05\n    50\t\n    51\t#### Formula Error Prevention\n    52\t- Verify all cell references are correct\n    53\t- Check for off-by-one errors in ranges\n    54\t- Ensure consistent formulas across all projection periods\n    55\t- Test with edge cases (zero values, negative numbers)\n    56\t- Verify no unintended circular references\n    57\t\n    58\t#### Documentation Requirements for Hardcodes\n    59\t- Comment or in cells beside (if end of table). Format: \"Source: [System/Document], [Date], [Specific Reference], [URL if applicable]\"\n    60\t- Examples:\n    61\t  - \"Source: Company 10-K, FY2024, Page 45, Revenue Note, [SEC EDGAR URL]\"\n    62\t  - \"Source: Company 10-Q, Q2 2025, Exhibit 99.1, [SEC EDGAR URL]\"\n    63\t  - \"Source: Bloomberg Terminal, 8/15/2025, AAPL US Equity\"\n    64\t  - \"Source: FactSet, 8/20/2025, Consensus Estimates Screen\"\n    65\t\n    66\t# XLSX creation, editing, and analysis\n    67\t\n    68\t## Overview\n    69\t\n    70\tA user may ask you to create, edit, or analyze the contents of an .xlsx file. You have different tools and workflows available for different tasks.\n    71\t\n    72\t## Important Requirements\n    73\t\n    74\t**LibreOffice Required for Formula Recalculation**: You can assume LibreOffice is installed for recalculating formula values using the `scripts/recalc.py` script. The script automatically configures LibreOffice on first run, including in sandboxed environments where Unix sockets are restricted (handled by `scripts/office/soffice.py`)\n    75\t\n    76\t## Reading and analyzing data\n    77\t\n    78\t### Data analysis with pandas\n    79\tFor data analysis, visualization, and basic operations, use **pandas** which provides powerful data manipulation capabilities:\n    80\t\n    81\t```python\n    82\timport pandas as pd\n    83\t\n    84\t# Read Excel\n    85\tdf = pd.read_excel('file.xlsx')  # Default: first sheet\n    86\tall_sheets = pd.read_excel('file.xlsx', sheet_name=None)  # All sheets as dict\n    87\t\n    88\t# Analyze\n    89\tdf.head()      # Preview data\n    90\tdf.info()      # Column info\n    91\tdf.describe()  # Statistics\n    92\t\n    93\t# Write Excel\n    94\tdf.to_excel('output.xlsx', index=False)\n    95\t```\n    96\t\n    97\t## Excel File Workflows\n    98\t\n    99\t## CRITICAL: Use Formulas, Not Hardcoded Values\n   100\t\n   101\t**Always use Excel formulas instead of calculating values in Python and hardcoding them.** This ensures the spreadsheet remains dynamic and updateable.\n   102\t\n   103\t### \u274c WRONG - Hardcoding Calculated Values\n   104\t```python\n   105\t# Bad: Calculating in Python and hardcoding result\n   106\ttotal = df['Sales'].sum()\n   107\tsheet['B10'] = total  # Hardcodes 5000\n   108\t\n   109\t# Bad: Computing growth rate in Python\n   110\tgrowth = (df.iloc[-1]['Revenue'] - df.iloc[0]['Revenue']) / df.iloc[0]['Revenue']\n   111\tsheet['C5'] = growth  # Hardcodes 0.15\n   112\t\n   113\t# Bad: Python calculation for average\n   114\tavg = sum(values) / len(values)\n   115\tsheet['D20'] = avg  # Hardcodes 42.5\n   116\t```\n   117\t\n   118\t### \u2705 CORRECT - Using Excel Formulas\n   119\t```python\n   120\t# Good: Let Excel calculate the sum\n   121\tsheet['B10'] = '=SUM(B2:B9)'\n   122\t\n   123\t# Good: Growth rate as Excel formula\n   124\tsheet['C5'] = '=(C4-C2)/C2'\n   125\t\n   126\t# Good: Average using Excel function\n   127\tsheet['D20'] = '=AVERAGE(D2:D19)'\n   128\t```\n   129\t\n   130\tThis applies to ALL calculations - totals, percentages, ratios, differences, etc. The spreadsheet should be able to recalculate when source data changes.\n   131\t\n   132\t## Common Workflow\n   133\t1. **Choose tool**: pandas for data, openpyxl for formulas/formatting\n   134\t2. **Create/Load**: Create new workbook or load existing file\n   135\t3. **Modify**: Add/edit data, formulas, and formatting\n   136\t4. **Save**: Write to file\n   137\t5. **Recalculate formulas (MANDATORY IF USING FORMULAS)**: Use the scripts/recalc.py script\n   138\t   ```bash\n   139\t   python scripts/recalc.py output.xlsx\n   140\t   ```\n   141\t6. **Verify and fix any errors**: \n   142\t   - The script returns JSON with error details\n   143\t   - If `status` is `errors_found`, check `error_summary` for specific error types and locations\n   144\t   - Fix the identified errors and recalculate again\n   145\t   - Common errors to fix:\n   146\t     - `#REF!`: Invalid cell references\n   147\t     - `#DIV/0!`: Division by zero\n   148\t     - `#VALUE!`: Wrong data type in formula\n   149\t     - `#NAME?`: Unrecognized formula name\n   150\t\n   151\t### Creating new Excel files\n   152\t\n   153\t```python\n   154\t# Using openpyxl for formulas and formatting\n   155\tfrom openpyxl import Workbook\n   156\tfrom openpyxl.styles import Font, PatternFill, Alignment\n   157\t\n   158\twb = Workbook()\n   159\tsheet = wb.active\n   160\t\n   161\t# Add data\n   162\tsheet['A1'] = 'Hello'\n   163\tsheet['B1'] = 'World'\n   164\tsheet.append(['Row', 'of', 'data'])\n   165\t\n   166\t# Add formula\n   167\tsheet['B2'] = '=SUM(A1:A10)'\n   168\t\n   169\t# Formatting\n   170\tsheet['A1'].font = Font(bold=True, color='FF0000')\n   171\tsheet['A1'].fill = PatternFill('solid', start_color='FFFF00')\n   172\tsheet['A1'].alignment = Alignment(horizontal='center')\n   173\t\n   174\t# Column width\n   175\tsheet.column_dimensions['A'].width = 20\n   176\t\n   177\twb.save('output.xlsx')\n   178\t```\n   179\t\n   180\t### Editing existing Excel files\n   181\t\n   182\t```python\n   183\t# Using openpyxl to preserve formulas and formatting\n   184\tfrom openpyxl import load_workbook\n   185\t\n   186\t# Load existing file\n   187\twb = load_workbook('existing.xlsx')\n   188\tsheet = wb.active  # or wb['SheetName'] for specific sheet\n   189\t\n   190\t# Working with multiple sheets\n   191\tfor sheet_name in wb.sheetnames:\n   192\t    sheet = wb[sheet_name]\n   193\t    print(f\"Sheet: {sheet_name}\")\n   194\t\n   195\t# Modify cells\n   196\tsheet['A1'] = 'New Value'\n   197\tsheet.insert_rows(2)  # Insert row at position 2\n   198\tsheet.delete_cols(3)  # Delete column 3\n   199\t\n   200\t# Add new sheet\n   201\tnew_sheet = wb.create_sheet('NewSheet')\n   202\tnew_sheet['A1'] = 'Data'\n   203\t\n   204\twb.save('modified.xlsx')\n   205\t```\n   206\t\n   207\t## Recalculating formulas\n   208\t\n   209\tExcel files created or modified by openpyxl contain formulas as strings but not calculated values. Use the provided `scripts/recalc.py` script to recalculate formulas:\n   210\t\n   211\t```bash\n   212\tpython scripts/recalc.py <excel_file> [timeout_seconds]\n   213\t```\n   214\t\n   215\tExample:\n   216\t```bash\n   217\tpython scripts/recalc.py output.xlsx 30\n   218\t```\n   219\t\n   220\tThe script:\n   221\t- Automatically sets up LibreOffice macro on first run\n   222\t- Recalculates all formulas in all sheets\n   223\t- Scans ALL cells for Excel errors (#REF!, #DIV/0!, etc.)\n   224\t- Returns JSON with detailed error locations and counts\n   225\t- Works on both Linux and macOS\n   226\t\n   227\t## Formula Verification Checklist\n   228\t\n   229\tQuick checks to ensure formulas work correctly:\n   230\t\n   231\t### Essential Verification\n   232\t- [ ] **Test 2-3 sample references**: Verify they pull correct values before building full model\n   233\t- [ ] **Column mapping**: Confirm Excel columns match (e.g., column 64 = BL, not BK)\n   234\t- [ ] **Row offset**: Remember Excel rows are 1-indexed (DataFrame row 5 = Excel row 6)\n   235\t\n   236\t### Common Pitfalls\n   237\t- [ ] **NaN handling**: Check for null values with `pd.notna()`\n   238\t- [ ] **Far-right columns**: FY data often in columns 50+ \n   239\t- [ ] **Multiple matches**: Search all occurrences, not just first\n   240\t- [ ] **Division by zero**: Check denominators before using `/` in formulas (#DIV/0!)\n   241\t- [ ] **Wrong references**: Verify all cell references point to intended cells (#REF!)\n   242\t- [ ] **Cross-sheet references**: Use correct format (Sheet1!A1) for linking sheets\n   243\t\n   244\t### Formula Testing Strategy\n   245\t- [ ] **Start small**: Test formulas on 2-3 cells before applying broadly\n   246\t- [ ] **Verify dependencies**: Check all cells referenced in formulas exist\n   247\t- [ ] **Test edge cases**: Include zero, negative, and very large values\n   248\t\n   249\t### Interpreting scripts/recalc.py Output\n   250\tThe script returns JSON with error details:\n   251\t```json\n   252\t{\n   253\t  \"status\": \"success\",           // or \"errors_found\"\n   254\t  \"total_errors\": 0,              // Total error count\n   255\t  \"total_formulas\": 42,           // Number of formulas in file\n   256\t  \"error_summary\": {              // Only present if errors found\n   257\t    \"#REF!\": {\n   258\t      \"count\": 2,\n   259\t      \"locations\": [\"Sheet1!B5\", \"Sheet1!C10\"]\n   260\t    }\n   261\t  }\n   262\t}\n   263\t```\n   264\t\n   265\t## Best Practices\n   266\t\n   267\t### Library Selection\n   268\t- **pandas**: Best for data analysis, bulk operations, and simple data export\n   269\t- **openpyxl**: Best for complex formatting, formulas, and Excel-specific features\n   270\t\n   271\t### Working with openpyxl\n   272\t- Cell indices are 1-based (row=1, column=1 refers to cell A1)\n   273\t- Use `data_only=True` to read calculated values: `load_workbook('file.xlsx', data_only=True)`\n   274\t- **Warning**: If opened with `data_only=True` and saved, formulas are replaced with values and permanently lost\n   275\t- For large files: Use `read_only=True` for reading or `write_only=True` for writing\n   276\t- Formulas are preserved but not evaluated - use scripts/recalc.py to update values\n   277\t\n   278\t### Working with pandas\n   279\t- Specify data types to avoid inference issues: `pd.read_excel('file.xlsx', dtype={'id': str})`\n   280\t- For large files, read specific columns: `pd.read_excel('file.xlsx', usecols=['A', 'C', 'E'])`\n   281\t- Handle dates properly: `pd.read_excel('file.xlsx', parse_dates=['date_column'])`\n   282\t\n   283\t## Code Style Guidelines\n   284\t**IMPORTANT**: When generating Python code for Excel operations:\n   285\t- Write minimal, concise Python code without unnecessary comments\n   286\t- Avoid verbose variable names and redundant operations\n   287\t- Avoid unnecessary print statements\n   288\t\n   289\t**For Excel files themselves**:\n   290\t- Add comments to cells with complex formulas or important assumptions\n   291\t- Document data sources for hardcoded values\n   292\t- Include notes for key calculations and model sections",
